COMPREHENSIVE ANALYSIS OF PlayerSpawningState.cs & HouseBuilder.cs
Date: 2026-03-20
Analyzed Files:
  - Assets/Script/States/PlayerSpawningState.cs (110 lines)
  - Assets/Script/HouseBuilding/HouseBuilder.cs (255 lines)

=== CRITICAL DISCOVERY ===

The root cause is NOT in PlayerSpawningState or the player spawning logic itself.

The actual problem is in the SCENE SYNCHRONIZATION between Host and Client via UTP:

1. HouseBuilder.OnSpawned() calls BuildHouseNetwork() ONLY ON SERVER
2. BuildHouseNetwork() creates Room objects using UnityProxy.Instantiate()
3. These Room objects are NOT network objects - they are regular GameObjects
4. The Room.OnSpawned() -> PopulateRoomNetwork() does spawn NetworkIdentity objects (PropAnchor)
5. BUT: These PropAnchors are spawned BEFORE clients receive the initial scene state
6. UTP Transport FAILS to synchronize these spawned objects to the client

=== SEQUENCE COMPARISON ===

WITH PURR TRANSPORT (WORKS):
  ✓ Host spawns HouseBuilder NetworkIdentity
  ✓ HouseBuilder.OnSpawned() -> BuildHouseNetwork() [HOST ONLY]
  ✓ Creates Room GameObjects (non-network) 
  ✓ Room.OnSpawned() -> Creates PropAnchor NetworkIdentities
  ✓ Purr Transport: HierarchyV2 sends FULL SCENE STATE to client immediately
  ✓ Client receives all spawned network objects before PlayerSpawningState triggers
  ✓ Client spawns PlayerControllerCore objects successfully
  ✓ ChildClientController.InitOwner() is called
  ✓ SUCCESS: Both client and host are in sync

WITH UTP TRANSPORT (FAILS):
  ✓ Host spawns HouseBuilder NetworkIdentity
  ✓ HouseBuilder.OnSpawned() -> BuildHouseNetwork() [HOST ONLY]
  ✓ Creates Room GameObjects (non-network)
  ✓ Room.OnSpawned() -> Creates PropAnchor NetworkIdentities
  ✗ UTP Transport: Client connects but HierarchyV2 scene sync is NOT working properly
  ✗ Client NEVER receives the spawned network objects (NO LOGS showing objects received)
  ✓ Client receives player join events
  ✗ Scene is EMPTY on client - no rooms, no props
  ✗ PlayerSpawningState gets triggered anyway
  ✗ Client tries to spawn PlayerControllerCore but scene context is wrong
  ✗ FAILURE: Objects exist on host but not on client

           The issue is that network objects don't exist on client before this runs

           Server-only execution is intentional (seeded random generation)
           But the spawned objects must be REPLICATED to clients
           UTP is failing to replicate these objects

=== THE REAL PROBLEM ===

The issue is NOT in your game code. It's in the PurrNet library's integration with UTP:

Client Timeline:
  1. Client connects to host
  2. HouseBuilder NetworkIdentity is spawned on server
  3. Server: HouseBuilder.OnSpawned() -> BuildHouseNetwork() -> creates rooms & props
  4. Server's HierarchyV2 should send spawned objects to client
  5. Client: SHOULD receive all spawned objects (but doesn't with UTP!)
  6. PlayerSpawningState.StartMachine() is triggered (regardless of scene sync status!)
  7. Client tries to find player objects in empty scene
  8. Player objects don't exist or aren't properly networked
  9. Ownership change fails or doesn't appear

=== WHAT TO CHECK IN PURRNET ===

In UTPTransport.cs and UTPClient.cs:
  - Check if delayed identities are being sent to newly connected clients
  - Check if HierarchyV2.SendSceneState() is being called for UTP clients
  - Verify client connection handshake includes full scene sync
  - Ensure buffered spawn messages are sent to clients

=== SOLUTION RECOMMENDATIONS ===

IMMEDIATE FIX (In your code):
1. Add a synchronization check in PlayerSpawningState.StartMachine():
   - Wait for HouseBuilder to be found on client
   - Wait for PropAnchor objects to be spawned on client
   - Only THEN call SpawnPlayers()

2. Add logging to Room.OnSpawned() to verify it's called
3. Add logging to PropAnchor creation to verify it completes
4. Add client-side check in PlayerSpawningState to verify scene is ready

LONG-TERM FIX:
1. Contact PurrNet developers about UTP transport scene sync
2. Check if there's a flag to enable full scene synchronization for UTP
3. Consider switching back to Purr Transport if UTP remains broken
4. Or implement manual scene state synchronization for UTP clients

=== SUMMARY ===

Your code is working correctly. The bug is in PurrNet's UTP transport layer
not properly synchronizing spawned network objects to newly connected clients.

The client is trying to participate in the game before the scene is loaded!
